# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
the derivative is the gradient of the tangent at that point. Deduced as the gradient
of a line passing through the point and a always closer other point where h tends to 0 ^9HGUROnI

function is concave up (smiling) means the derivative goes from negative to positive, so
always growing, so the second derivative is always positive, so you also have a local min ^VGwqzudw

opposite for concave down ^iWkiLreZ

in case of local point of inflection the concavity changes, the derivative is first increasing than decreasing or
vice versa except when it touches 0, the second derivative goes from negative to positive or opposite ^Spc61AeZ
